# big-code-cross-k8s-arch-001: Kubernetes CRD Lifecycle (Cross-Repo)

## Task

Trace how a Custom Resource Definition (CRD) flows through the Kubernetes ecosystem: from CRD type definitions and validation, through etcd storage and the dynamic HTTP handler, to the generated client, informers, listers, and the dynamic client. Map the complete lifecycle across four logical sub-projects within the Kubernetes monorepo.

## Context

- **Repository**: kubernetes/kubernetes (Go, ~2.5M LOC)
- **Category**: Architectural Understanding (cross-repo)
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/, staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/, staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/, staging/src/k8s.io/api/

## Architecture Overview

Kubernetes uses a staging directory structure where four logically separate projects coexist in one monorepo:

1. **apiextensions-apiserver** — CRD type definitions, validation, etcd storage, dynamic HTTP handler
2. **client-go** — Generated typed clients, informers, listers, and the dynamic client
3. **apimachinery** — Runtime scheme, GVK/GVR types, ObjectMeta, Unstructured representation
4. **api** — Internal hub types and group registration

## Requirements

1. Trace the CRD type definition layer: internal hub types, external v1 types, and Scheme registration
2. Map the server-side lifecycle: validation, etcd storage, and the dynamic customresource_handler
3. Trace the client-side access layer: typed clientset, SharedIndexInformer, Lister, and DynamicClient
4. Identify the foundational types in apimachinery that everything depends on: Scheme, GVK/GVR, TypeMeta/ObjectMeta, Unstructured

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```
## Files Examined
- path/to/file1.ext — role in architecture
- path/to/file2.ext — role in architecture
...

## Dependency Chain
1. Foundation: apimachinery types (Scheme, GVK, ObjectMeta, Unstructured)
2. Type definitions: apiextensions types (internal hub + external v1 + registration)
3. Server-side: validation -> etcd storage -> HTTP handler
4. Client-side: typed client -> informer -> lister -> dynamic client
...

## Analysis
[Detailed architectural analysis including:
- Cross-project dependency flow
- How CRD types bridge the four sub-projects
- The role of Scheme and GVK in type registration
- How Unstructured enables dynamic custom resource access
- The checkpoint between server-side storage and client-side informer caching]

## Summary
[Concise 2-3 sentence summary of the CRD lifecycle across the K8s ecosystem]
```

## Evaluation Criteria

- File recall: Did you find files across ALL four sub-projects?
- Dependency accuracy: Did you trace the correct cross-project dependency chain?
- Architectural coherence: Did you identify how the sub-projects integrate?

## What Was Written

### Section 1 — Type Definitions
Traces the full type hierarchy from apimachinery primitives (`GroupVersionKind`, `GroupVersionResource`, `Scheme`, `TypeMeta`, `ObjectMeta`, `Unstructured`) through the apiextensions-apiserver internal hub type (`CustomResourceDefinition`, `CustomResourceDefinitionSpec`, `CustomResourceDefinitionVersion`, `CustomResourceConversion`, etc.) to the v1 versioned type and scheme registration via `install.Install(scheme)`.

### Section 2 — Validation
Covers the four top-level validation entry points (`ValidateCustomResourceDefinition`, `ValidateCustomResourceDefinitionUpdate`, `ValidateCustomResourceDefinitionStoredVersions`, `ValidateUpdateCustomResourceDefinitionStatus`), the `validationOptions` struct that controls enforcement, OpenAPI schema validation, CEL `x-kubernetes-validations` with `CELSchemaContext` / `TotalCost` / `preexistingExpressions` ratcheting, and CR instance validation (the five-step chain in `customResourceStrategy.Validate`).

### Section 3 — etcd Storage
Documents the CRD registry (`REST` embedding `genericregistry.Store`, finalizer-based deletion via `GuaranteedUpdate`, `statusStrategy`), the CR registry (`CustomResourceStorage` with `Unstructured`-backed store, `StatusREST`, `ScaleREST`), and the two lifecycle controllers (`NamingConditionController` → `NamesAccepted`, `EstablishingController` → `Established`).

### Section 4 — HTTP Handler

  "command": "create",
  "file_text": "# CRD Lifecycle Across the Kubernetes Monorepo: Architectural Analysis\n\n## Overview\n\nA CustomResourceDefinition (CRD) is the mechanism by which Kubernetes allows users to extend the API with new resource types. Its lifecycle spans four sub-projects in the Kubernetes monorepo staging tree:\n\n| Sub-project | Staging path | Role |\n|---|---|---|\n| **apimachinery** | `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery` | Core type primitives, runtime scheme, unstructured representation |\n| **apiextensions-apiserver** | `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver` | CRD type definitions, validation, etcd storage, HTTP handler, typed clients, informers, listers |\n| **client-go** | `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go` | Shared informer/cache infrastructure, dynamic client |\n| **api** | `staging/src/k8s.io/api` | Built-in API types (referenced by CRD scale subresource via `autoscaling/v1.Scale`) |\n\nThe sections below trace each architectural layer in the order a CRD object travels through the system: from its Go type definition, through admission and validation, into etcd, out through the HTTP handler, and finally to the client-side machinery that watches and caches it.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Type Definitions\n\n### 1.1 apimachinery Primitives\n\nEvery Kubernetes object is identified by a **GroupVersionKind** (GVK) and addressed as a **GroupVersionResource** (GVR). These are defined in:\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/schema/group_version.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype GroupVersionKind  struct { Group, Version, Kind string }\ntype GroupVersionResource struct { Group, Version, Resource string }\ntype GroupVersion struct { Group, Version string }\n```\n\nThe **Scheme** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/scheme.go`) is the central registry that maps Go types to GVKs:\n\n```go\ntype Scheme struct {\n    gvkToType map[schema.GroupVersionKind]reflect.Type\n    typeToGVK map[reflect.Type][]schema.GroupVersionKind\n    // ...\n}\n```\n\n`AddKnownTypes(gv GroupVersion, types ...Object)` and `AddKnownTypeWithName(gvk GVK, obj Object)` populate these maps. Every API group calls these at init time so the runtime can encode/decode objects by GVK.\n\nAll API objects embed two apimachinery structs (`staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go`):\n\n```go\ntype TypeMeta struct {\n    Kind       string `json:\"kind,omitempty\"`\n    APIVersion string `json:\"apiVersion,omitempty\"`\n}\ntype ObjectMeta struct { /* Name, Namespace, UID, ResourceVersion, Labels, Annotations, Finalizers, ... */ }\n```\n\nThe **Unstructured** type (`staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/unstructured/unstructured.go`) is the universal container for objects whose Go type is not known at compile time:\n\n```go\ntype Unstructured struct {\n    Object map[string]interface{}\n}\n```\n\nIt implements `metav1.Object` and `runtime.Unstructured`. `UnstructuredContent()` returns the raw map. Custom resource instances are always stored and served as `*unstructured.Unstructured` inside the apiextensions-apiserver.\n\n### 1.2 Internal Hub Type (apiextensions-apiserver)\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go\n```\n\nThe **internal hub version** is the canonical in-memory representation used by all server-side logic. Versioned objects (v1, v1beta1) are converted to/from this hub before any processing.\n\n```go\ntype CustomResourceDefinition struct {\n    metav1.TypeMeta\n    metav1.ObjectMeta\n    Spec   CustomResourceDefinitionSpec\n    Status CustomResourceDefinitionStatus\n}\n\ntype CustomResourceDefinitionSpec struct {\n    Group                string\n    Version              string                          // deprecated single-version field\n    Versions             []CustomResourceDefinitionVersion\n    Names                CustomResourceDefinitionNames\n    Scope                ResourceScope                   // \"Cluster\" | \"Namespaced\"\n    Validation           *CustomResourceValidation       // top-level schema (deprecated)\n    Subresources         *CustomResourceSubresources\n    AdditionalPrinterColumns []CustomResourceColumnDefinition\n    SelectableFields     []SelectableField\n    Conversion           *CustomResourceConversion\n    PreserveUnknownFields bool\n}\n\ntype CustomResourceDefinitionVersion struct {\n    Name               string\n    Served             bool\n    Storage            bool\n    Deprecated         bool\n    DeprecationWarning *string\n    Schema             *CustomResourceValidation\n    Subresources       *CustomResourceSubresources\n    AdditionalPrinterColumns []CustomResourceColumnDefinition\n    SelectableFields   []SelectableField\n}\n\ntype CustomResourceDefinitionNames struct {\n    Plural, Singular string\n    ShortNames       []string\n    Kind, ListKind   string\n    Categories       []string\n}\n\ntype CustomResourceDefinitionStatus struct {\n    Conditions    []CustomResourceDefinitionCondition\n    AcceptedNames CustomResourceDefinitionNames\n    StoredVersions []string\n}\n\ntype CustomResourceConversion struct {\n    Strategy                ConversionStrategyType // \"None\" | \"Webhook\"\n    WebhookClientConfig     *WebhookClientConfig\n    ConversionReviewVersions []string\n}\n\ntype CustomResourceValidation struct {\n    OpenAPIV3Schema *JSONSchemaProps\n}\n\ntype CustomResourceSubresources struct {\n    Status *CustomResourceSubresourceStatus\n    Scale  *CustomResourceSubresourceScale\n}\n```\n\nThe constant `CustomResourceCleanupFinalizer = \"customresourcecleanup.apiextensions.k8s.io\"` is placed on a CRD when deletion is requested, ensuring all CR instances are garbage-collected before the CRD itself is removed.\n\n### 1.3 Versioned v1 Type\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go\n```\n\nThe v1 type mirrors the internal hub field-for-field. Conversion functions in `v1/conversion.go` handle the mapping between the two representations, including the flattening/unflattening of the deprecated top-level `Validation`/`Subresources` fields into per-version entries.\n\n### 1.4 Scheme Registration\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/install/install.go\n```\n\n```go\nfunc Install(scheme *runtime.Scheme) {\n    internal.Install(scheme)   // registers hub types under APIVersionInternal\n    v1beta1.Install(scheme)    // registers v1beta1 types\n    v1.Install(scheme)         // registers v1 types\n    scheme.SetVersionPriority(v1.SchemeGroupVersion, v1beta1.SchemeGroupVersion)\n}\n```\n\nEach `Install` calls `AddKnownTypes` for `CustomResourceDefinition` and `CustomResourceDefinitionList`, and `AddToGroupVersion` for the standard discovery types. The priority order (v1 > v1beta1) controls which version is preferred for encoding responses.\n\nThe internal group is registered under `GroupVersion{Group: \"apiextensions.k8s.io\", Version: runtime.APIVersionInternal}` while v1 uses `GroupVersion{Group: \"apiextensions.k8s.io\", Version: \"v1\"}`.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Validation\n\n### 2.1 CRD Structural Validation\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go\n```\n\nThe top-level entry points are:\n\n| Function | Called by | Purpose |\n|---|---|---|\n| `ValidateCustomResourceDefinition(ctx, obj)` | `strategy.Validate` on create | Full static validation |\n| `ValidateCustomResourceDefinitionUpdate(ctx, obj, oldObj)` | `strategy.ValidateUpdate` on update | Update-specific checks + ratcheting |\n| `ValidateCustomResourceDefinitionStoredVersions(...)` | Status update path | Ensures stored versions are consistent |\n| `ValidateUpdateCustomResourceDefinitionStatus(obj, oldObj)` | `statusStrategy.ValidateUpdate` | Status-only update validation |\n\n`ValidateCustomResourceDefinition` builds a `validationOptions` struct that controls which checks are enforced:\n\n```go\ntype validationOptions struct {\n    requireOpenAPISchema        bool\n    requireValidPropertyType    bool\n    requireStructuralSchema     bool\n    requireAtomicSetType        bool\n    requireMapListKeysMaxProperties bool\n    preexistingExpressions      preexistingExpressions\n    suppressPerExpressionCost   bool\n    celEnvironmentSet           *environment.EnvSet\n}\n```\n\n`validateCustomResourceDefinitionSpec` (line 342) validates:\n- Group name format (DNS subdomain)\n- Version name format\n- Names (plural, singular, kind, listKind, categories, shortNames)\n- Scope value\n- Conversion configuration (webhook URL/service reference, CABundle, review versions)\n- Per-version schema via `validateCustomResourceDefinitionVersion`\n\n`ValidateCustomResourceDefinitionOpenAPISchema` (line 980) validates the JSONSchemaProps tree, checking:\n- Valid property types (string, integer, number, boolean, array, object)\n- No `$ref` in structural schemas\n- Correct use of `additionalProperties`, `allOf`, `anyOf`, `oneOf`, `not`\n- `x-kubernetes-list-type` / `x-kubernetes-list-map-keys` consistency\n- `x-kubernetes-map-type` values\n\n### 2.2 CEL Validation (x-kubernetes-validations)\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/types_jsonschema.go\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/cel_validation.go\n```\n\nEach `JSONSchemaProps` node may carry:\n\n```go\nXValidations ValidationRules  // []ValidationRule\n```\n\n```go\ntype ValidationRule struct {\n    Rule              string  // CEL expression; `self` is bound to the scoped value\n    Message           string\n    MessageExpression string  // CEL expression producing the error message\n    Reason            metav1.StatusReason\n    FieldPath         string  // relative JSON path for error attribution\n    OptionalOldSelf   *bool   // enables transition rules on optional fields\n}\n```\n\n`CELSchemaContext` (in `cel_validation.go`) lazily computes `CELTypeInfo` for each schema node that has `x-kubernetes-validations`. Type info is derived either cheaply from the parent's type info via a `typeInfoAccessor`, or expensively by converting the JSONSchemaProps to a CEL type via a `converter`. A `TotalCost` accumulator enforces the aggregate cost limit across all rules in a CRD.\n\nDuring CRD create/update validation, `findPreexistingExpressions` identifies CEL expressions that existed before the update; `suppressExpressionCostForUnchangedSchema` relaxes per-expression cost limits for unchanged schema versions, preventing spurious rejections when cost estimation improves across Kubernetes versions.\n\n### 2.3 Structural Schema\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/structural.go\n```\n\n`structuralschema.NewStructural(jsonSchemaProps)` converts a `JSONSchemaProps` tree into a `Structural` tree:\n\n```go\ntype Structural struct {\n    Items      *Structural\n    Properties map[string]Structural\n    Generic                  // type, nullable, default, ...\n    Extensions               // x-kubernetes-* extensions\n    ValueValidation          // enum, format, minimum, maximum, pattern, ...\n}\n```\n\nThe structural schema is the internal representation used for pruning, defaulting, and CEL evaluation at request time. It is computed once per CRD version in `getOrCreateServingInfoFor` and cached in `crdInfo`.\n\n### 2.4 CR Instance Validation\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/strategy.go\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/validator.go\n```\n\n`customResourceStrategy.Validate` (line 204) chains:\n1. `ValidateTypeMeta` \u2014 checks `apiVersion` and `kind` fields\n2. `ValidateObjectMetaAccessor` \u2014 standard ObjectMeta validation (name format, label syntax, etc.)\n3. `ValidateCustomResource` \u2014 OpenAPI schema validation against the structural schema\n4. `schemaobjectmeta.Validate` \u2014 validates embedded ObjectMeta fields in the CR body\n5. `structurallisttype.ValidateListSetsAndMaps` \u2014 validates `x-kubernetes-list-type=set/map` invariants\n6. `celValidator.Validate` \u2014 evaluates all `x-kubernetes-validations` CEL rules\n\n`ValidateUpdate` additionally performs ratcheting: list-type and CEL validations are skipped for fields whose values have not changed, preventing updates from being rejected due to pre-existing invalid data.\n\n---\n\n## 3. etcd Storage\n\n### 3.1 CRD Registry\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresourcedefinition/etcd.go\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresourcedefinition/strategy.go\n```\n\n`REST` embeds `*genericregistry.Store`, which provides the standard CRUD operations backed by etcd via the `storage.Interface` abstraction:\n\n```go\ntype REST struct {\n    *genericregistry.Store\n}\n```\n\n`NewREST` wires the store:\n\n```go\nstore := &genericregistry.Store{\n    NewFunc:                  func() runtime.Object { return &apiextensions.CustomResourceDefinition{} },\n    NewListFunc:              func() runtime.Object { return &apiextensions.CustomResourceDefinitionList{} },\n    PredicateFunc:            MatchCustomResourceDefinition,\n    DefaultQualifiedResource: apiextensions.Resource(\"customresourcedefinitions\"),\n    CreateStrategy:           strategy,\n    UpdateStrategy:           strategy,\n    DeleteStrategy:           strategy,\n    ResetFieldsStrategy:      strategy,\n    TableConvertor:           rest.NewDefaultTableConvertor(...),\n}\nstore.CompleteWithOptions(options)  // wires etcd backend, codec, key prefix\n```\n\n**Finalizer-based deletion** (`REST.Delete`, line 84): When a CRD is first deleted, `Delete` intercepts the call and uses `GuaranteedUpdate` to atomically add the `customresourcecleanup.apiextensions.k8s.io` finalizer before delegating to the standard delete path. The `CRDFinalizer` controller (`pkg/controller/finalizer/crd_finalizer.go`) watches for CRDs with this finalizer, deletes all CR instances via `ListerCollectionDeleter`, then removes the finalizer to allow the CRD object itself to be garbage-collected.\n\n**Strategy** (`strategy.go`):\n\n```go\n// strategy (cluster-scoped)\nfunc (s strategy) NamespaceScoped() bool { return false }\n\nfunc (s strategy) PrepareForCreate(ctx, obj) {\n    // sets Status.StoredVersions from Spec.Versions[*].Storage=true\n    // drops disabled fields\n}\n\nfunc (s strategy) PrepareForUpdate(ctx, obj, old) {\n    // preserves Status; drops disabled fields\n}\n\nfunc (s strategy) Validate(ctx, obj) field.ErrorList {\n    return validation.ValidateCustomResourceDefinition(ctx, obj.(*apiextensions.CustomResourceDefinition))\n}\n\nfunc (s strategy) ValidateUpdate(ctx, obj, old) field.ErrorList {\n    return validation.ValidateCustomResourceDefinitionUpdate(ctx, obj, old)\n}\n```\n\n**StatusStrategy** (`statusStrategy`, line 178): `PrepareForUpdate` preserves the Spec (only Status changes are allowed), and `ValidateUpdate` calls `ValidateUpdateCustomResourceDefinitionStatus`.\n\n**NamingConditionController** (`pkg/controller/status/naming_controller.go`): Watches all CRDs in a group and sets the `NamesAccepted` condition by detecting plural/singular/kind/shortName conflicts across CRDs in the same group. Once `NamesAccepted=True`, the **EstablishingController** (`pkg/controller/establish/establishing_controller.go`) sets `Established=True`, making the CRD's API endpoints active.\n\n### 3.2 Custom Resource Registry\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/etcd.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype CustomResourceStorage struct {\n    CustomResource *REST\n    Status         *StatusREST\n    Scale          *ScaleREST\n}\n```\n\n`NewStorage` builds a `genericregistry.Store` where `NewFunc` and `NewListFunc` return `*unstructured.Unstructured` and `*unstructured.UnstructuredList` respectively \u2014 the store is entirely schema-agnostic at the Go type level:\n\n```go\nNewFunc: func() runtime.Object {\n    ret := &unstructured.Unstructured{}\n    ret.SetGroupVersionKind(kind)\n    return ret\n},\nNewListFunc: func() runtime.Object {\n    ret := &unstructured.UnstructuredList{}\n    ret.SetGroupVersionKind(listKind)\n    return ret\n},\n```\n\n**StatusREST**: A separate store copy with `CreateStrategy=nil`, `DeleteStrategy=nil`, and `UpdateStrategy=statusStrategy`. `statusStrategy.PrepareForUpdate` preserves the Spec, allowing only `.status` mutations.\n\n**ScaleREST**: Implements `rest.Patcher` and `rest.GroupVersionKindProvider`. `GroupVersionKind` always returns `autoscaling/v1.Scale`. `Get` reads the CR and extracts the replica count from the JSON path specified in `CustomResourceSubresourceScale.SpecReplicasPath`. `Update` writes back to the same path.\n\n---\n\n## 4. HTTP Handler\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go\n```\n\n### 4.1 Handler Structure\n\n`crdHandler` is the `http.Handler` that serves all custom resource API endpoints:\n\n```go\ntype crdHandler struct {\n    versionDiscoveryHandler *versionDiscoveryHandler\n    groupDiscoveryHandler   *groupDiscoveryHandler\n    customStorage           atomic.Value          // holds crdStorageMap\n    customStorageLock       sync.Mutex\n    crdLister               listers.CustomResourceDefinitionLister\n    delegate                http.Handler\n    restOptionsGetter       generic.RESTOptionsGetter\n    admission               admission.Interface\n    establishingController  *establish.EstablishingController\n    converterFactory        *conversion.CRConverterFactory\n    authorizer              authorizer.Authorizer\n    requestTimeout          time.Duration\n    staticOpenAPISpec       map[string]*spec.Schema\n    maxRequestBodyBytes     int64\n    // ...\n}\n```\n\n`crdStorageMap` maps CRD UID to `*crdInfo`:\n\n```go\ntype crdStorageMap map[types.UID]*crdInfo\n\ntype crdInfo struct {\n    spec               *apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinitionSpec\n    acceptedNames      *apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinitionNames\n    deprecated         map[string]bool\n    warnings           map[string][]string\n    storages           map[string]customresource.CustomResourceStorage  // keyed by version\n    requestScopes      map[string]*handlers.RequestScope\n    statusRequestScopes map[string]*handlers.RequestScope\n    scaleRequestScopes  map[string]*handlers.RequestScope\n    storageVersion     string\n    waitGroup          *utilwaitgroup.SafeWaitGroup\n}\n```\n\nThe `customStorage` field is an `atomic.Value` holding a `crdStorageMap`. Reads are lock-free (atomic load); writes use `customStorageLock` and copy-on-write semantics, making the common read path extremely fast.\n\n### 4.2 Request Routing\n\n`ServeHTTP` (line 223) parses the request URL into a `RequestInfo`, looks up the CRD by group/resource/version, and dispatches:\n\n```\nServeHTTP\n  \u2514\u2500 getOrCreateServingInfoFor(crd.UID, crd.Name) \u2192 *crdInfo\n       \u251c\u2500 serveResource  \u2192 handlers.GetResource / CreateResource / UpdateResource / DeleteResource / ...\n       \u251c\u2500 serveStatus    \u2192 handlers.GetResource / UpdateResource (status subresource)\n       \u2514\u2500 serveScale     \u2192 handlers.GetResource / UpdateResource (scale subresource)\n```\n\nEach path selects the appropriate `CustomResourceStorage` and `RequestScope` from `crdInfo.storages[version]` and `crdInfo.requestScopes[version]`.\n\n### 4.3 Lazy Storage Creation\n\n`getOrCreateServingInfoFor` (line 605) implements double-checked locking:\n\n1. Atomic load of `crdStorageMap`; return cached `crdInfo` if present (fast path, no lock).\n2. Acquire `customStorageLock`.\n3. Re-fetch the CRD from the lister (to observe any concurrent updates).\n4. Atomic load again; return if another goroutine already created it.\n5. Build new `crdInfo`:\n   - For each served version: convert the v1 schema to internal, call `structuralschema.NewStructural`, prune defaults via `structuraldefaulting.PruneDefaults`.\n   - Build OpenAPI models for SSA via `buildOpenAPIModelsForApply`.\n   - Create `managedfields.TypeConverter` (schema-aware or deduced).\n   - Call `converterFactory.NewConverter(crd)` to get safe/unsafe `runtime.ObjectConvertor` (None or Webhook).\n   - For each version: call `customresource.NewStorage(...)` to create `CustomResourceStorage`.\n   - Build `handlers.RequestScope` for main, status, and scale endpoints.\n   - Wire `scopeWithFieldManager` for SSA support.\n6. Atomic store of updated `crdStorageMap`.\n\n### 4.4 Storage Invalidation\n\nThe handler registers event handlers on the CRD informer at construction time:\n\n```go\ncrdInformer.Informer().AddEventHandler(cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{\n    AddFunc:    ret.createCustomResourceDefinition,\n    UpdateFunc: ret.updateCustomResourceDefinition,\n    DeleteFunc: func(obj interface{}) { /* remove from map */ },\n})\n```\n\n`updateCustomResourceDefinition` (line 467) compares the new CRD's spec and acceptedNames against the cached `crdInfo`. If they differ, it removes the stale entry from the map (copy-on-write) and calls `tearDown` in a goroutine. `tearDown` waits for in-flight requests to drain via `crdInfo.waitGroup`, then calls `storage.CustomResource.DestroyFunc()` to release etcd connections and caches.\n\n### 4.5 Serialization Pipeline\n\n`unstructuredNegotiatedSerializer` (line 1074) is a custom `runtime.NegotiatedSerializer` that wraps the standard JSON/YAML/Protobuf serializers. Its `DecoderToVersion` method returns a `schemaCoercingDecoder` that applies:\n\n1. **Pruning** (`structuralpruning.PruneWithOptions`): removes fields not present in the structural schema (unless `x-kubernetes-preserve-unknown-fields` is set).\n2. **Defaulting** (`structuraldefaulting.Default`): fills in `default` values from the schema.\n3. **ObjectMeta coercion**: validates embedded ObjectMeta fields.\n\n`unstructuredCreator.New(gvk)` always returns a fresh `*unstructured.Unstructured`, so the server never needs a registered Go type for CR instances.\n\n### 4.6 Version Conversion\n\n`CRConverterFactory` (`pkg/apiserver/conversion/converter.go`) produces a `crConverter` that implements `runtime.ObjectConvertor`:\n\n- **None strategy**: `Convert` copies the object and updates `apiVersion` in the unstructured map.\n- **Webhook strategy**: `webhookConverterFactory.NewWebhookConverter(crd)` builds a converter that sends a `ConversionReview` request to the webhook endpoint (URL or in-cluster Service reference), receives the converted objects, and validates the response.\n\nThe converter is used by the versioning codec inside `unstructuredNegotiatedSerializer` to convert stored objects to the requested API version on read, and to convert request bodies to the storage version on write.\n\n### 4.7 Server-Side Apply (SSA)\n\n`scopeWithFieldManager` (line 1037) calls `managedfields.NewDefaultCRDFieldManager` with the `TypeConverter` built from the CRD's OpenAPI models. This wires the `FieldManager` into the `RequestScope`, enabling SSA semantics (field ownership tracking via `managedFields` in ObjectMeta) for all CR PATCH requests with `Content-Type: application/apply-patch+yaml`.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Typed Clients\n\n### 5.1 Clientset\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/clientset/clientset/clientset.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype Interface interface {\n    Discovery() discovery.DiscoveryInterface\n    ApiextensionsV1() apiextensionsv1.ApiextensionsV1Interface\n    ApiextensionsV1beta1() apiextensionsv1beta1.ApiextensionsV1beta1Interface\n}\n\ntype Clientset struct {\n    *discovery.DiscoveryClient\n    apiextensionsV1      *apiextensionsv1.ApiextensionsV1Client\n    apiextensionsV1beta1 *apiextensionsv1beta1.ApiextensionsV1beta1Client\n}\n```\n\n`NewForConfig` constructs a `rest.Config` copy, creates per-group REST clients, and wires the `DiscoveryClient`. The clientset is code-generated by `client-gen`.\n\n### 5.2 Typed CRD Client\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/clientset/clientset/typed/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype CustomResourceDefinitionInterface interface {\n    Create(ctx, *v1.CustomResourceDefinition, metav1.CreateOptions) (*v1.CustomResourceDefinition, error)\n    Update(ctx, *v1.CustomResourceDefinition, metav1.UpdateOptions) (*v1.CustomResourceDefinition, error)\n    UpdateStatus(ctx, *v1.CustomResourceDefinition, metav1.UpdateOptions) (*v1.CustomResourceDefinition, error)\n    Delete(ctx, name string, metav1.DeleteOptions) error\n    DeleteCollection(ctx, metav1.DeleteOptions, metav1.ListOptions) error\n    Get(ctx, name string, metav1.GetOptions) (*v1.CustomResourceDefinition, error)\n    List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions) (*v1.CustomResourceDefinitionList, error)\n    Watch(ctx, metav1.ListOptions) (watch.Interface, error)\n    Patch(ctx, name string, pt types.PatchType, data []byte, metav1.PatchOptions, subresources ...string) (*v1.CustomResourceDefinition, error)\n    Apply(ctx, *apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinitionApplyConfiguration, metav1.ApplyOptions) (*v1.CustomResourceDefinition, error)\n    ApplyStatus(ctx, *apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinitionApplyConfiguration, metav1.ApplyOptions) (*v1.CustomResourceDefinition, error)\n}\n```\n\nThe concrete `customResourceDefinitions` struct holds a `*ApiextensionsV1Client` (which wraps a `rest.Interface`). Every method serializes the typed `v1.CustomResourceDefinition` to JSON, issues the HTTP request, and deserializes the response back to the typed struct. `Apply` converts `metav1.ApplyOptions` to `metav1.PatchOptions` and issues a PATCH with `types.ApplyPatchType` (`application/apply-patch+yaml`).\n\n---\n\n## 6. Informers\n\n### 6.1 CRD Informer (apiextensions-apiserver)\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/informers/externalversions/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype CustomResourceDefinitionInformer interface {\n    Informer() cache.SharedIndexInformer\n    Lister() v1.CustomResourceDefinitionLister\n}\n```\n\n`NewFilteredCustomResourceDefinitionInformer` constructs a `cache.SharedIndexInformer` backed by a `cache.ListWatch`:\n\n```go\ncache.NewSharedIndexInformer(\n    &cache.ListWatch{\n        ListFunc:  func(opts) { return client.ApiextensionsV1().CustomResourceDefinitions().List(ctx, opts) },\n        WatchFunc: func(opts) { return client.ApiextensionsV1().CustomResourceDefinitions().Watch(ctx, opts) },\n    },\n    &apiextensionsv1.CustomResourceDefinition{},  // example object for type detection\n    resyncPeriod,\n    indexers,\n)\n```\n\n`customResourceDefinitionInformer.Informer()` calls `factory.InformerFor(...)` which deduplicates informers by type \u2014 multiple callers share a single `SharedIndexInformer` and its underlying watch connection.\n\n`customResourceDefinitionInformer.Lister()` calls `v1.NewCustomResourceDefinitionLister(f.Informer().GetIndexer())`, wiring the lister directly to the informer's in-memory index.\n\n### 6.2 SharedIndexInformer Internals (client-go)\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/tools/cache/shared_informer.go\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/tools/cache/reflector.go\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/tools/cache/delta_fifo.go\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/tools/cache/store.go\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/tools/cache/index.go\n```\n\nThe `sharedIndexInformer` (line 358) has three main components:\n\n```\nsharedIndexInformer\n  \u251c\u2500 controller Controller\n  \u2502    \u2514\u2500 Reflector\n  \u2502         \u251c\u2500 ListerWatcher (ListWatch)\n  \u2502         \u2514\u2500 DeltaFIFO (store)\n  \u251c\u2500 indexer Indexer (ThreadSafeStore)\n  \u2514\u2500 processor *sharedProcessor (fan-out to event handlers)\n```\n\n**Reflector** (`reflector.go`, line 53):\n\n```go\ntype Reflector struct {\n    expectedType    reflect.Type\n    expectedGVK     *schema.GroupVersionKind\n    store           Store          // the DeltaFIFO\n    listerWatcher   ListerWatcher\n    // backoff, resync, error handler, ...\n}\n```\n\n`ListAndWatch` performs an initial List (populating the store via `Replace`), then opens a Watch stream. Each watch event is dispatched to the DeltaFIFO as an `Added`, `Modified`, or `Deleted` delta. On watch error, the reflector backs off and restarts.\n\n**DeltaFIFO** (`delta_fifo.go`, line 101):\n\n```go\ntype DeltaFIFO struct {\n    items map[string]Deltas   // key \u2192 []Delta\n    queue []string            // ordered keys\n    // ...\n}\n\ntype DeltaType string\n// Added | Updated | Deleted | Replaced | Sync\n```\n\nThe DeltaFIFO is a producer-consumer queue. The Reflector produces deltas; the controller's `processLoop` consumes them by calling `Pop`, which blocks until a delta is available, then calls `HandleDeltas`.\n\n**HandleDeltas** (`sharedIndexInformer`): For each delta, updates the local `Indexer` (add/update/delete) and distributes the event to all registered `ResourceEventHandler` listeners via the `sharedProcessor`. Listeners receive `OnAdd`, `OnUpdate`, or `OnDelete` callbacks.\n\n**Store / Indexer interfaces** (`store.go`, `index.go`):\n\n```go\ntype Store interface {\n    Add(obj interface{}) error\n    Update(obj interface{}) error\n    Delete(obj interface{}) error\n    List() []interface{}\n    ListKeys() []string\n    Get(obj interface{}) (item interface{}, exists bool, err error)\n    GetByKey(key string) (item interface{}, exists bool, err error)\n    Replace([]interface{}, string) error\n    Resync() error\n}\n\ntype Indexer interface {\n    Store\n    Index(indexName string, obj interface{}) ([]interface{}, error)\n    IndexKeys(indexName, indexedValue string) ([]string, error)\n    ListIndexFuncValues(indexName string) []string\n    ByIndex(indexName, indexedValue string) ([]interface{}, error)\n    GetIndexers() Indexers\n    AddIndexers(newIndexers Indexers) error\n}\n```\n\nThe concrete implementation is `ThreadSafeStore` backed by a `map[string]interface{}` with secondary indexes (e.g., `cache.NamespaceIndex` \u2192 `cache.MetaNamespaceIndexFunc`).\n\n---\n\n## 7. Listers\n\n### 7.1 Typed CRD Lister\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/listers/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype CustomResourceDefinitionLister interface {\n    List(selector labels.Selector) (ret []*v1.CustomResourceDefinition, err error)\n    Get(name string) (*v1.CustomResourceDefinition, error)\n    CustomResourceDefinitionListerExpansion\n}\n\ntype customResourceDefinitionLister struct {\n    indexer cache.Indexer\n}\n```\n\n`List` calls `cache.ListAll(s.indexer, selector, ...)` which iterates the indexer's key set and applies the label selector. `Get` calls `s.indexer.GetByKey(name)` (CRDs are cluster-scoped, so the key is just the name). Both methods return read-only pointers; callers must not mutate the returned objects.\n\nThe lister is code-generated by `lister-gen` and is always backed by the informer's `Indexer`, making all reads local (no network calls).\n\n### 7.2 Dynamic Lister\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/interface.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype Lister interface {\n    List(selector labels.Selector) (ret []*unstructured.Unstructured, err error)\n    Get(name string) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n    Namespace(namespace string) NamespaceLister\n}\n\ntype NamespaceLister interface {\n    List(selector labels.Selector) (ret []*unstructured.Unstructured, err error)\n    Get(name string) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n}\n```\n\n`dynamicLister{indexer cache.Indexer, gvr schema.GroupVersionResource}` implements `Lister`. `Get` uses `indexer.GetByKey(name)` for cluster-scoped resources. `dynamicNamespaceLister.Get` uses `indexer.GetByKey(namespace + \"/\" + name)`. Both return `*unstructured.Unstructured`, making the dynamic lister GVR-parameterized but type-agnostic.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Dynamic Client\n\n### 8.1 Interface\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/interface.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype Interface interface {\n    Resource(resource schema.GroupVersionResource) NamespaceableResourceInterface\n}\n\ntype NamespaceableResourceInterface interface {\n    Namespace(namespace string) ResourceInterface\n    ResourceInterface\n}\n\ntype ResourceInterface interface {\n    Create(ctx, *unstructured.Unstructured, metav1.CreateOptions, subresources ...string) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n    Update(ctx, *unstructured.Unstructured, metav1.UpdateOptions, subresources ...string) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n    UpdateStatus(ctx, *unstructured.Unstructured, metav1.UpdateOptions) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n    Delete(ctx, name string, metav1.DeleteOptions, subresources ...string) error\n    DeleteCollection(ctx, metav1.DeleteOptions, metav1.ListOptions) error\n    Get(ctx, name string, metav1.GetOptions, subresources ...string) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n    List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions) (*unstructured.UnstructuredList, error)\n    Watch(ctx, metav1.ListOptions) (watch.Interface, error)\n    Patch(ctx, name string, pt types.PatchType, data []byte, metav1.PatchOptions, subresources ...string) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n    Apply(ctx, name string, *unstructured.Unstructured, metav1.ApplyOptions, subresources ...string) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n    ApplyStatus(ctx, name string, *unstructured.Unstructured, metav1.ApplyOptions) (*unstructured.Unstructured, error)\n}\n```\n\n### 8.2 Implementation\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/simple.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype DynamicClient struct {\n    client rest.Interface\n}\n\ntype dynamicResourceClient struct {\n    client    *DynamicClient\n    resource  schema.GroupVersionResource\n    namespace string\n}\n```\n\n`DynamicClient.Resource(gvr)` returns a `&dynamicResourceClient{resource: gvr}`. `Namespace(ns)` returns a copy with `namespace` set.\n\nAll write methods follow the same pattern:\n1. Encode the `*unstructured.Unstructured` to JSON bytes via `runtime.Encode(unstructured.UnstructuredJSONScheme, obj)`.\n2. Build the REST request (POST/PUT/PATCH) with the appropriate URL segments.\n3. Execute the request and read the response body.\n4. Decode the response via `runtime.Decode(unstructured.UnstructuredJSONScheme, retBytes)`.\n5. Type-assert to `*unstructured.Unstructured`.\n\n`Apply` converts `metav1.ApplyOptions` to `metav1.PatchOptions` and issues a PATCH with `types.ApplyPatchType`. `ApplyStatus` delegates to `Apply` with `\"status\"` as a subresource.\n\n`Watch` sets `opts.Watch = true` and issues a GET, receiving a streaming response decoded by the watch decoder into `watch.Event` values.\n\n`makeURLSegments` constructs the URL path: for namespaced resources, `/apis/{group}/{version}/namespaces/{namespace}/{resource}/{name}`; for cluster-scoped, `/apis/{group}/{version}/{resource}/{name}`.\n\n### 8.3 Dynamic Informer\n\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go\n```\n\n```go\ntype DynamicSharedInformerFactory interface {\n    ForResource(resource schema.GroupVersionResource) informers.GenericInformer\n    Start(stopCh <-chan struct{})\n    WaitForCacheSync(stopCh <-chan struct{}) map[schema.GroupVersionResource]bool\n    Shutdown()\n}\n```\n\n`dynamicSharedInformerFactory` maintains a `map[schema.GroupVersionResource]informers.GenericInformer`. `ForResource(gvr)` returns a cached informer or creates one via `NewFilteredDynamicInformer`:\n\n```go\nfunc NewFilteredDynamicInformer(client dynamic.Interface, gvr GVR, namespace string, ...) informers.GenericInformer {\n    return &dynamicInformer{\n        informer: cache.NewSharedIndexInformer(\n            &cache.ListWatch{\n                ListFunc:  func(opts) { return client.Resource(gvr).Namespace(namespace).List(ctx, opts) },\n                WatchFunc: func(opts) { return client.Resource(gvr).Namespace(namespace).Watch(ctx, opts) },\n            },\n            &unstructured.Unstructured{},  // example object\n            resyncPeriod,\n            indexers,\n        ),\n        gvr: gvr,\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThe `ListWatch` uses the dynamic client, so the informer works for any GVR without compile-time type knowledge. The example object `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` tells the Reflector to expect unstructured objects. `dynamicInformer.Lister()` returns a `cache.GenericLister` backed by the informer's indexer, which wraps a `dynamicLister`.\n\n---\n\n## End-to-End Lifecycle Summary\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502                          CRD LIFECYCLE                                      \u2502\n\u2502                                                                             \u2502\n\u2502  1. Versioned objects are converted at the API boundary. This isolates version-specific concerns (field renames, deprecations) from business logic.\n\n2. **Unstructured at the CR layer**: Custom resource instances are never represented as typed Go structs inside the server. `*unstructured.Unstructured` is the universal container, validated against the structural schema at runtime.\n\n3. **Lazy, copy-on-write storage map**: `crdHandler.customStorage` uses `atomic.Value` for lock-free reads and copy-on-write writes, ensuring that the hot path (serving CR requests) is never blocked by CRD updates.\n\n4. **Informer-driven invalidation**: The HTTP handler does not poll etcd for CRD changes. It registers event handlers on the CRD informer, which is itself backed by the same watch machinery used by all other controllers. This creates a consistent, event-driven invalidation model.\n\n5. **Finalizer-based garbage collection**: The `customresourcecleanup.apiextensions.k8s.io` finalizer ensures that CR instances are always deleted before the CRD is removed, preventing orphaned resources.\n\n6. **Shared cache infrastructure**: Both typed informers (generated by `informer-gen`) and dynamic informers (`DynamicSharedInformerFactory`) use the identical `SharedIndexInformer` / `Reflector` / `DeltaFIFO` / `ThreadSafeStore` stack from `client-go/tools/cache`. The only difference is the Go type of the cached objects (`*v1.CustomResourceDefinition` vs `*unstructured.Unstructured`) and the `ListerWatcher` implementation.\n",
